SELECT t.booked_ticket_id, t.booked_at, t.user_id, t0.booked_ticket_detail_id, t0.booked_ticket_id, t0.quantity, t0.ticket_code, t0.ticket_code0, t0.category_id, t0.event_date, t0.price, t0.quota, t0.ticket_name, t0.category_id0, t0.category_name

    FROM bookedticket AS b
    WHERE b.booked_ticket_id = @__bookedTicketId_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT b0.booked_ticket_detail_id, b0.booked_ticket_id, b0.quantity, b0.ticket_code, t1.ticket_code AS ticket_code0, t1.category_id, t1.event_date, t1.price, t1.quota, t1.ticket_name, c.category_id AS category_id0, c.category_name

FROM (

    FROM ticket AS t

) AS t0
